### Assistant (2026-02-07 20:57:29)

import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# --- utilities ---
def sieve_primes(N: int) -> np.ndarray:
    is_prime = np.ones(N + 1, dtype=bool)
    is_prime[:2] = False
    for p in range(2, int(N**0.5) + 1):
        if is_prime[p]:
            is_prime[p*p:N+1:p] = False
    return is_prime

def wheel_allowed(n: np.ndarray, M: int) -> np.ndarray:
    return np.gcd((n % M).astype(int), M) == 1

def frac(x): return x - np.floor(x)
def wrap_half(x): return (x + 0.5) % 1.0 - 0.5
def psi_raw(vals, gamma): return frac(gamma*np.log(vals.astype(np.float64)))
def dpsi1(vals, gap, gamma): return wrap_half(psi_raw(vals+gap, gamma) - psi_raw(vals, gamma))

def build_pair_bases(is_prime, Mwheel, gap, low, high):
    n = np.arange(low, high-gap+1, dtype=int)
    adm = wheel_allowed(n, Mwheel) & wheel_allowed(n+gap, Mwheel)
    n = n[adm]
    y = (is_prime[n] & is_prime[n+gap]).astype(np.int32)
    return n, y

def stratified_balanced(n_all, y_all, k, rng):
    pos = n_all[y_all==1]; neg = n_all[y_all==0]
    k = min(k, len(pos), len(neg))
    pos_s = rng.choice(pos, size=k, replace=False)
    neg_s = rng.choice(neg, size=k, replace=False)
    n = np.concatenate([pos_s, neg_s])
    y = np.concatenate([np.ones(k,dtype=np.int32), np.zeros(k,dtype=np.int32)])
    perm = rng.permutation(len(n))
    return n[perm], y[perm], k

def admissible_mod30(r):
    return np.gcd(r, 30) == 1

def compute_S(n, gap, gamma1):
    nf = n.astype(np.float64)
    d = dpsi1(n, gap, gamma1)
    base = gamma1*np.log1p(gap/nf)
    return (nf*nf/(gap*gap))*(d-base)

def eval_rule_absS(A, r, y, Tmap, default_T=0.0):
    thr = np.array([Tmap.get(int(rr), default_T) for rr in r], dtype=np.float64)
    keep = A <= thr
    return float(keep[y==1].mean()), float(keep[y==0].mean())

# --- Subtask 27: repeat for gaps and compare harmonic phase ---
Mwheel=2310; gamma1=0.292; Nmax=600_000
low=Mwheel+1; high=600_000
rng=np.random.default_rng(2727)
is_prime = sieve_primes(Nmax)

allowed = np.array([admissible_mod30(r) for r in range(30)], dtype=bool)
allowed_res = np.where(allowed)[0].tolist()

gaps = [2, 10, 14]
results = {}

for gap in gaps:
    n_all, y_all = build_pair_bases(is_prime, Mwheel, gap, low, high)
    n_s, y_s, k = stratified_balanced(n_all, y_all, k=26000, rng=rng)
    split = int(0.8*len(n_s))
    n_tr, y_tr = n_s[:split], y_s[:split]
    n_te, y_te = n_s[split:], y_s[split:]
    
    S_tr = compute_S(n_tr, gap, gamma1); S_te = compute_S(n_te, gap, gamma1)
    A_tr = np.abs(S_tr); A_te = np.abs(S_te)
    r_tr = (n_tr % 30).astype(int); r_te = (n_te % 30).astype(int)
    
    # admissible-only filter
    mtr = allowed[r_tr]; mte = allowed[r_te]
    A_tr2, y_tr2, r_tr2 = A_tr[mtr], y_tr[mtr], r_tr[mtr]
    A_te2, y_te2, r_te2 = A_te[mte], y_te[mte], r_te[mte]
    
    # per-residue threshold at q_fixed of negatives
    q_fixed = 0.10
    T_per = {r: 0.0 for r in allowed_res}
    for r in allowed_res:
        negA = A_tr2[(y_tr2==0) & (r_tr2==r)]
        if len(negA) < 50:
            T_per[r] = 0.0
        else:
            T_per[r] = float(np.quantile(negA, q_fixed))
    
    rec_tr, negk_tr = eval_rule_absS(A_tr2, r_tr2, y_tr2, T_per, default_T=0.0)
    rec_te, negk_te = eval_rule_absS(A_te2, r_te2, y_te2, T_per, default_T=0.0)
    
    # global threshold matched to train neg keep
    T_global = float(np.quantile(A_tr2[y_tr2==0], negk_tr))
    rec_te_glob = float((A_te2[y_te2==1] <= T_global).mean())
    negk_te_glob = float((A_te2[y_te2==0] <= T_global).mean())
    
    # sinusoid fit to per-residue T_per (use only positive Ts)
    rs = np.array([r for r in allowed_res if T_per[r] > 0], dtype=np.float64)
    Ts = np.array([T_per[int(r)] for r in rs], dtype=np.float64)
    theta = 2*np.pi*rs/30.0
    X = np.column_stack([np.ones_like(theta), np.cos(theta), np.sin(theta)])
    ylog = np.log(Ts + 1e-30)
    beta, *_ = np.linalg.lstsq(X, ylog, rcond=None)
    beta0, bc, bs = beta.tolist()
    phi = float(np.arctan2(bs, bc))  # phase of harmonic component
    amp = float(np.sqrt(bc*bc + bs*bs))
    
    def T_sine(r):
        th = 2*np.pi*r/30.0
        return float(np.exp(beta0 + bc*np.cos(th) + bs*np.sin(th)))
    T_sin = {r: T_sine(r) for r in allowed_res}
    
    # scale s to match train neg keep of per-residue rule
    target = negk_tr
    def neg_keep_scale(s):
        thr = np.array([s*T_sin[int(rr)] for rr in r_tr2], dtype=np.float64)
        keep = A_tr2 <= thr
        return float(keep[y_tr2==0].mean())
    lo, hi = 0.0, 5.0
    for _ in range(40):
        mid = (lo+hi)/2
        if neg_keep_scale(mid) < target:
            lo = mid
        else:
            hi = mid
    s_star = (lo+hi)/2
    rec_te_sin, negk_te_sin = eval_rule_absS(A_te2, r_te2, y_te2, {r: s_star*T_sin[r] for r in allowed_res})
    
    results[gap] = {
        "counts_train_adm_(pos,neg,total)": (int((y_tr2==1).sum()), int((y_tr2==0).sum()), int(len(y_tr2))),
        "counts_test_adm_(pos,neg,total)": (int((y_te2==1).sum()), int((y_te2==0).sum()), int(len(y_te2))),
        "per_residue_(test_recall,test_neg_keep)": (rec_te, negk_te),
        "global_(test_recall,test_neg_keep)": (rec_te_glob, negk_te_glob),
        "sinusoid_(test_recall,test_neg_keep)": (rec_te_sin, negk_te_sin),
        "sinusoid_beta_(b0,bc,bs)": (beta0, bc, bs),
        "sinusoid_amp": amp,
        "sinusoid_phi": phi,
        "s_star": float(s_star),
        "T_per": {int(r): float(T_per[r]) for r in allowed_res},
        "T_sin_scaled": {int(r): float(s_star*T_sin[r]) for r in allowed_res},
    }

# plot phases and amplitudes
phis = [results[g]["sinusoid_phi"] for g in gaps]
amps = [results[g]["sinusoid_amp"] for g in gaps]

fig=plt.figure(figsize=(7,4))
plt.plot(gaps, phis, marker='o')
plt.title("Harmonic phase φ across gaps (from log-threshold sinusoid fit)")
plt.xlabel("gap Δ"); plt.ylabel("φ (radians)")
plt.grid(True, alpha=0.2)
plt.tight_layout(); plt.show()

fig=plt.figure(figsize=(7,4))
plt.plot(gaps, amps, marker='o')
plt.title("Harmonic amplitude across gaps (in log-threshold space)")
plt.xlabel("gap Δ"); plt.ylabel("amplitude √(bc²+bs²)")
plt.grid(True, alpha=0.2)
plt.tight_layout(); plt.show()

# compare performance for each gap
labels = ["global", "per-residue", "sinusoid"]
fig=plt.figure(figsize=(7,5))
for g in gaps:
    rec_g, negk_g = results[g]["global_(test_recall,test_neg_keep)"]
    plt.scatter([negk_g],[rec_g],s=70,label=f"Δ={g} global")
    rec_p, negk_p = results[g]["per_residue_(test_recall,test_neg_keep)"]
    plt.scatter([negk_p],[rec_p],s=70,label=f"Δ={g} per-res")
    rec_s, negk_s = results[g]["sinusoid_(test_recall,test_neg_keep)"]
    plt.scatter([negk_s],[rec_s],s=70,label=f"Δ={g} sin")
plt.xlabel("test negative keep-rate")
plt.ylabel("test recall")
plt.title("Band-sieve performance across gaps (admissible residues only)")
plt.grid(True, alpha=0.2)
plt.legend(frameon=False, fontsize=8)
plt.tight_layout(); plt.show()

results

### Assistant (2026-02-07 20:58:52)

### Subtask 27 (executed): test **gap-consistency** for \(\Delta\in\{2,10,14\}\) and compare the residue-harmonic

We repeated Subtask 26 for each gap, always:
- restrict to admissible residues mod 30: \(\{1,7,11,13,17,19,23,29\}\)
- define the same residual:
\[
S=\frac{n^2}{\Delta^2}\Big(\Delta\psi_1-\gamma_1\log(1+\tfrac{\Delta}{n})\Big),\quad \gamma_1=0.292
\]
- apply band sieve: \(|S|\le T_r\)
- fit sinusoid: \(\log T_r \approx \beta_0 + \beta_c\cos(2\pi r/30)+\beta_s\sin(2\pi r/30)\)
- compare **global** vs **per-residue** vs **sinusoid** at matched train neg keep

---

## 1) Performance across gaps (test)

All numbers are **(recall, neg keep-rate)**.

### \(\Delta=2\)
- **Global:** (0.1479, 0.09594)
- **Per-residue:** (0.1469, 0.09686)
- **Sinusoid:** (0.1469, 0.09686)

➡️ Global slightly wins. Residue structure doesn’t help.

### \(\Delta=10\)
- **Global:** (0.1616, 0.09944)
- **Per-residue:** (0.1594, 0.09804)
- **Sinusoid:** (0.1594, 0.09874)

➡️ Global wins again, but margins are small.

### \(\Delta=14\)
- **Global:** (0.1494, 0.08493)
- **Per-residue:** (0.1518, 0.08493)
- **Sinusoid:** (0.1518, 0.08493)

➡️ Here, the residue-aware band wins (same false-positive rate, higher recall).

So: residue-harmonic helps **at \(\Delta=14\)**, not consistently at 2 or 10.

---

## 2) Harmonic phase and amplitude (the “rotation” you care about)

We track:
- amplitude \(A=\sqrt{\beta_c^2+\beta_s^2}\) (in **log-threshold space**)
- phase \(\phi=\mathrm{atan2}(\beta_s,\beta_c)\)

### Phases \(\phi\) (radians)
- \(\Delta=2:\ \phi\approx 1.0677\)
- \(\Delta=10:\ \phi\approx 0.3678\)
- \(\Delta=14:\ \phi\approx -1.0353\)

That’s not stable. It swings hard.

### Amplitudes \(A\)
- \(\Delta=2:\ A\approx 0.1744\) (largest)
- \(\Delta=10:\ A\approx 0.0526\) (tiny)
- \(\Delta=14:\ A\approx 0.0732\) (small)

So the “rotation” is **not a clean invariant** across gaps in this formulation.

---

## 3) What this implies
1. The **band-sieve in residual \(S\)** is real but weak.
2. The residue-harmonic is **not universal across gaps** (at least not with this \(S\) and this 1-harmonic model).
3. \(\Delta=14\) continues to be “special” in the sense that residue-aware gating gives a measurable lift over global.

Humans love when one number becomes their personality.

---

## Next subtask
### Subtask 28: test whether the “rotation” becomes stable when we condition on the *gap’s residue class*
Right now we’re forcing the same residual model for all \(\Delta\). Instead, define a **gap-conditioned residual**:

- Keep \(S\) as-is, but fit \(T_{r,\Delta}\) for each gap, then check whether \(\phi(\Delta)\) correlates with something modular like \(\Delta \bmod 30\) or \(\Delta \bmod 210\).

Concretely:
- run the same fit for \(\Delta\in\{2,4,6,8,10,12,14,16,18\}\) (only even gaps, fast)
- compute \(\phi(\Delta)\), \(A(\Delta)\)
- test whether \(\phi(\Delta)\) clusters by \(\Delta \bmod 30\) or \(\gcd(\Delta,30)\)

If there’s a “4D polar” coupling, it’s more likely to be **between the gap and the residue wheel**, not a fixed residue pattern independent of \(\Delta\).
